### Summary

The party navigated desert combat and coordinated a complex ascent of the Cinder Hold.

**Combat and Narrative Cutscenes**  
The group fought animated armor and swords while managing cutscenes involving a prisoner. Players utilized healing abilities and spells to overcome encounter threats and replenish their health.

**Second Encounter and Strategy**  
The party engaged a second wave of animated objects and zombie Heragon. They opted for stealth to bypass certain threats while coordinating defensive formations.

**Cinder Hold Ascent**  
The group successfully climbed the Cinder Hold using shared climbing gear and magical assistance. They reached the entrance platform and prepared to investigate the nearby prison cells.

### Next steps

- [ ] \[The group\] Research Spell: Review spell duration and implications of Sarin's magic ending. Investigate options for continued spell application.

- [ ] \[Phillyp Henning\] Fix Character Sheet: Correct Jinx's spell list and inventory tools. Ensure character sheet configuration is accurate.

- [ ] \[Phillyp Henning\] Fix Armor: Resolve low AC calculation for Jinx's artificer armor. Investigate appropriate armor types post-session completion.

Emily C confirmed they would not need to climb as they were flying ([02:41:49](#02:41:49)). D offered to give up their advantage and single damage negation from their climbing gear so that everyone else could benefit from the one-time fall damage protection ([02:42:29](#02:42:29)).

Phillyp Henning proposed that Lindsay’s support would grant the group a re-roll on their checks, effectively catching people if they slipped ([02:48:02](#02:48:02)).

* **Initial Climbing Check and Gear Strategy**: The group began their attempt to climb the Cinder Hold and were instructed to make an Acrobatics or Athletics check against a difficulty of 13\. Daniel Monteiro decided that their climbing gear would grant every person one-time save they could use, opting to "spread the love" rather than taking advantage for themself ([02:49:02](#02:49:02)).

* **Utilizing Enlarge for Strength Advantage**: The team discussed using the Enlarge ability to aid Daniel Monteiro in the climb, as it grants advantage on Strength checks and saving throws ([02:50:39](#02:50:39)). Phillyp Henning clarified that Daniel Monteiro, who has a Strength modifier of plus two, had to go up first to incur these bonuses for the others ([02:50:39](#02:50:39)).

* **Strategy for Using Climbing Resources**: The ascent strategy involved Daniel Monteiro leading the climb, utilizing the climbing gear to put down batons and rope, and the rest of the group splitting the resources of the climbing kit ([02:50:39](#02:50:39)). The decision was made for Daniel Monteiro to "go big," taking advantage on Strength checks from the Enlarge ability, and then head out ([02:52:00](#02:52:00)).

* **First Round of Ascent Checks and Failures**: The initial ascent checks were made, with Daniel Monteiro performing a Strength check with advantage and clearing the check ([02:52:00](#02:52:00)). A character named Jinx failed their check multiple times, which prompted the use of a reroll from Lindsay to prevent them from having to start the climb over again ([02:52:38](#02:52:38)).

* **Aiding Jinx's Climb**: After Jinx's repeated failures, Cas Vander Grift's character, Carrick, offered to put Jinx on their shoulders, which meant Carrick would take a minus two penalty on their athletics check. Carrick, whose athletics modifier is plus seven, took Jinx on their shoulder, and the climb resumed ([02:54:11](#02:54:11)).

* **Successful Ascent of Cinder Hold**: The party continued their climb, with checks for Daniel Monteiro, Sarin, and Carrick, and successfully reached an elevation of 90 feet ([02:54:55](#02:54:55)). Sarin required a reroll, which Lindsay provided, to successfully complete the final portion of the ascent ([02:56:52](#02:56:52)).

* **Reaching the Cinder Hold Platform**: The team successfully climbed the side of Cinder Hold, which was a challenging ascent described as climbing a massive tree. Due to their planning and the use of the darkness shroud, they were able to climb up to a platform created by the concave shape of Cinder Hold's body ([02:56:52](#02:56:52)).

* **Arrival and Conclusion of the Session**: Daniel Monteiro reached the platform first, followed by Sarin, Carrick, Jinx, and Lindsay, who all took a moment to recover from the 90-foot climb ([02:57:36](#02:57:36)).
